Chapter 1

Chapter 1

[1 NIV] In the beginning God created the heavens and the earth.
[1 KJV] In the beginning God created the heaven and the earth.
[2 NIV] Now the earth was [a] formless and empty, darkness was over the surface of the deep, and the Spirit of God was hovering over the waters.
[2 KJV] And the earth was without form, and void; and darkness was upon the face of the deep. And the Spirit of God moved upon the face of the waters.
[3 NIV] And God said, "Let there be light," and there was light.
[3 KJV] And God said, Let there be light: and there was light.
[4 NIV] God saw that the light was good, and he separated the light from the darkness.
[4 KJV] And God saw the light, that it was good: and God divided the light from the darkness.
[5 NIV] God called the light "day," and the darkness he called "night." And there was evening, and there was morning--the first day.
[5 KJV] And God called the light Day, and the darkness he called Night. And the evening and the morning were the first day.
[6 NIV] And God said, "Let there be an expanse between the waters to separate water from water."
[6 KJV] And God said, Let there be a firmament in the midst of the waters, and let it divide the waters from the waters.
[7 NIV] So God made the expanse and separated the water under the expanse from the water above it. And it was so.
[7 KJV] And God made the firmament, and divided the waters which were under the firmament from the waters which were above the firmament: and it was so.
[8 NIV] God called the expanse "sky." And there was evening, and there was morning--the second day.
[8 KJV] And God called the firmament Heaven. And the evening and the morning were the second day.
[9 NIV] And God said, "Let the water under the sky be gathered to one place, and let dry ground appear." And it was so.
[9 KJV] And God said, Let the waters under the heaven be gathered together unto one place, and let the dry land appear: and it was so.
[10 NIV] God called the dry ground "land," and the gathered waters he called "seas." And God saw that it was good.
[10 KJV] And God called the dry land Earth; and the gathering together of the waters called he Seas: and God saw that it was good.
[11 NIV] Then God said, "Let the land produce vegetation: seed-bearing plants and trees on the land that bear fruit with seed in it, according to their various kinds." And it was so.
[11 KJV] And God said, Let the earth bring forth grass, the herb yielding seed, and the fruit tree yielding fruit after his kind, whose seed is in itself, upon the earth: and it was so.
[12 NIV] The land produced vegetation: plants bearing seed according to their kinds and trees bearing fruit with seed in it according to their kinds. And God saw that it was good.
[12 KJV] And the earth brought forth grass, and herb yielding seed after his kind, and the tree yielding fruit, whose seed was in itself, after his kind: and God saw that it was good.
[13 NIV] And there was evening, and there was morning--the third day.
[13 KJV] And the evening and the morning were the third day.
[14 NIV] And God said, "Let there be lights in the expanse of the sky to separate the day from the night, and let them serve as signs to mark seasons and days and years,
[14 KJV] And God said, Let there be lights in the firmament of the heaven to divide the day from the night; and let them be for signs, and for seasons, and for days, and years:
[15 NIV] and let them be lights in the expanse of the sky to give light on the earth." And it was so.
[15 KJV] And let them be for lights in the firmament of the heaven to give light upon the earth: and it was so.
[16 NIV] God made two great lights--the greater light to govern the day and the lesser light to govern the night. He also made the stars.
[16 KJV] And God made two great lights; the greater light to rule the day, and the lesser light to rule the night: he made the stars also.
[17 NIV] God set them in the expanse of the sky to give light on the earth,
[17 KJV] And God set them in the firmament of the heaven to give light upon the earth,
[18 NIV] to govern the day and the night, and to separate light from darkness. And God saw that it was good.
[18 KJV] And to rule over the day and over the night, and to divide the light from the darkness: and God saw that it was good.
[19 NIV] And there was evening, and there was morning--the fourth day.
[19 KJV] And the evening and the morning were the fourth day.
[20 NIV] And God said, "Let the water teem with living creatures, and let birds fly above the earth across the expanse of the sky."
[20 KJV] And God said, Let the waters bring forth abundantly the moving creature that hath life, and fowl that may fly above the earth in the open firmament of heaven.
[21 NIV] So God created the great creatures of the sea and every living and moving thing with which the water teems, according to their kinds, and every winged bird according to its kind. And God saw that it was good.
[21 KJV] And God created great whales, and every living creature that moveth, which the waters brought forth abundantly, after their kind, and every winged fowl after his kind: and God saw that it was good.
[22 NIV] God blessed them and said, "Be fruitful and increase in number and fill the water in the seas, and let the birds increase on the earth."
[22 KJV] And God blessed them, saying, Be fruitful, and multiply, and fill the waters in the seas, and let fowl multiply in the earth.
[23 NIV] And there was evening, and there was morning--the fifth day.
[23 KJV] And the evening and the morning were the fifth day.
[24 NIV] And God said, "Let the land produce living creatures according to their kinds: livestock, creatures that move along the ground, and wild animals, each according to its kind." And it was so.
[24 KJV] And God said, Let the earth bring forth the living creature after his kind, cattle, and creeping thing, and beast of the earth after his kind: and it was so.
[25 NIV] God made the wild animals according to their kinds, the livestock according to their kinds, and all the creatures that move along the ground according to their kinds. And God saw that it was good.
[25 KJV] And God made the beast of the earth after his kind, and cattle after their kind, and every thing that creepeth upon the earth after his kind: and God saw that it was good.
[26 NIV] Then God said, "Let us make man in our image, in our likeness, and let them rule over the fish of the sea and the birds of the air, over the livestock, over all the earth, [b] and over all the creatures that move along the ground."
[26 KJV] And God said, Let us make man in our image, after our likeness: and let them have dominion over the fish of the sea, and over the fowl of the air, and over the cattle, and over all the earth, and over every creeping thing that creepeth upon the earth.
[27 NIV] So God created man in his own image, in the image of God he created him; male and female he created them.
[27 KJV] So God created man in his own image, in the image of God created he him; male and female created he them.
[28 NIV] God blessed them and said to them, "Be fruitful and increase in number; fill the earth and subdue it. Rule over the fish of the sea and the birds of the air and over every living creature that moves on the ground."
[28 KJV] And God blessed them, and God said unto them, Be fruitful, and multiply, and replenish the earth, and subdue it: and have dominion over the fish of the sea, and over the fowl of the air, and over every living thing that moveth upon the earth.
[29 NIV] Then God said, "I give you every seed-bearing plant on the face of the whole earth and every tree that has fruit with seed in it. They will be yours for food.
[29 KJV] And God said, Behold, I have given you every herb bearing seed, which is upon the face of all the earth, and every tree, in the which is the fruit of a tree yielding seed; to you it shall be for meat.
[30 NIV] And to all the beasts of the earth and all the birds of the air and all the creatures that move on the ground--everything that has the breath of life in it--I give every green plant for food." And it was so.
[30 KJV] And to every beast of the earth, and to every fowl of the air, and to every thing that creepeth upon the earth, wherein there is life, I have given every green herb for meat: and it was so.
[31 NIV] God saw all that he had made, and it was very good. And there was evening, and there was morning--the sixth day.
[31 KJV] And God saw every thing that he had made, and, behold, it was very good. And the evening and the morning were the sixth day.

b. [26] Hebrew; Syriac all the wild animals

Chapter 2

[1 NIV] Thus the heavens and the earth were completed in all their vast array.
[1 KJV] Thus the heavens and the earth were finished, and all the host of them.
[2 NIV] By the seventh day God had finished the work he had been doing; so on the seventh day he rested [a] from all his work.
[2 KJV] And on the seventh day God ended his work which he had made; and he rested on the seventh day from all his work which he had made.
[3 NIV] And God blessed the seventh day and made it holy, because on it he rested from all the work of creating that he had done.
[3 KJV] And God blessed the seventh day, and sanctified it: because that in it he had rested from all his work which God created and made.
[4 NIV] This is the account of the heavens and the earth when they were created. When the LORD God made the earth and the heavens--
[4 KJV] These are the generations of the heavens and of the earth when they were created, in the day that the LORD God made the earth and the heavens,
[5 NIV] and no shrub of the field had yet appeared on the earth [b] and no plant of the field had yet sprung up, for the LORD God had not sent rain on the earth [c] and there was no man to work the ground,
[5 KJV] And every plant of the field before it was in the earth, and every herb of the field before it grew: for the LORD God had not caused it to rain upon the earth, and there was not a man to till the ground.
[6 NIV] but streams [d] came up from the earth and watered the whole surface of the ground--
[6 KJV] But there went up a mist from the earth, and watered the whole face of the ground.
[7 NIV] the LORD God formed the man [e] from the dust of the ground and breathed into his nostrils the breath of life, and the man became a living being.
[7 KJV] And the LORD God formed man of the dust of the ground, and breathed into his nostrils the breath of life; and man became a living soul.
[8 NIV] Now the LORD God had planted a garden in the east, in Eden; and there he put the man he had formed.
[8 KJV] And the LORD God planted a garden eastward in Eden; and there he put the man whom he had formed.
[9 NIV] And the LORD God made all kinds of trees grow out of the ground--trees that were pleasing to the eye and good for food. In the middle of the garden were the tree of life and the tree of the knowledge of good and evil.
[9 KJV] And out of the ground made the LORD God to grow every tree that is pleasant to the sight, and good for food; the tree of life also in the midst of the garden, and the tree of knowledge of good and evil.
[10 NIV] A river watering the garden flowed from Eden; from there it was separated into four headwaters.
[10 KJV] And a river went out of Eden to water the garden; and from thence it was parted, and became into four heads.
[11 NIV] The name of the first is the Pishon; it winds through the entire land of Havilah, where there is gold.
[11 KJV] The name of the first is Pison: that is it which compasseth the whole land of Havilah, where there is gold;
[12 NIV] (The gold of that land is good; aromatic resin [f] and onyx are also there.)
[12 KJV] And the gold of that land is good: there is bdellium and the onyx stone.
[13 NIV] The name of the second river is the Gihon; it winds through the entire land of Cush. [g]
[13 KJV] And the name of the second river is Gihon: the same is it that compasseth the whole land of Ethiopia.
[14 NIV] The name of the third river is the Tigris; it runs along the east side of Asshur. And the fourth river is the Euphrates.
[14 KJV] And the name of the third river is Hiddekel: that is it which goeth toward the east of Assyria. And the fourth river is Euphrates.
[15 NIV] The LORD God took the man and put him in the Garden of Eden to work it and take care of it.
[15 KJV] And the LORD God took the man, and put him into the garden of Eden to dress it and to keep it.
[16 NIV] And the LORD God commanded the man, "You are free to eat from any tree in the garden;
[16 KJV] And the LORD God commanded the man, saying, Of every tree of the garden thou mayest freely eat:
[17 NIV] but you must not eat from the tree of the knowledge of good and evil, for when you eat of it you will surely die."
[17 KJV] But of the tree of the knowledge of good and evil, thou shalt not eat of it: for in the day that thou eatest thereof thou shalt surely die.
[18 NIV] The LORD God said, "It is not good for the man to be alone. I will make a helper suitable for him."
[18 KJV] And the LORD God said, It is not good that the man should be alone; I will make him an help meet for him.
[19 NIV] Now the LORD God had formed out of the ground all the beasts of the field and all the birds of the air. He brought them to the man to see what he would name them; and whatever the man called each living creature, that was its name.
[19 KJV] And out of the ground the LORD God formed every beast of the field, and every fowl of the air; and brought them unto Adam to see what he would call them: and whatsoever Adam called every living creature, that was the name thereof.
[20 NIV] So the man gave names to all the livestock, the birds of the air and all the beasts of the field. But for Adam [h] no suitable helper was found.
[20 KJV] And Adam gave names to all cattle, and to the fowl of the air, and to every beast of the field; but for Adam there was not found an help meet for him.
[21 NIV] So the LORD God caused the man to fall into a deep sleep; and while he was sleeping, he took one of the man's ribs [i] and closed up the place with flesh.
[21 KJV] And the LORD God caused a deep sleep to fall upon Adam, and he slept: and he took one of his ribs, and closed up the flesh instead thereof;
[22 NIV] Then the LORD God made a woman from the rib [j] he had taken out of the man, and he brought her to the man.
[22 KJV] And the rib, which the LORD God had taken from man, made he a woman, and brought her unto the man.
[23 NIV] The man said, "This is now bone of my bones and flesh of my flesh; she shall be called `woman, [k] ' for she was taken out of man."
[23 KJV] And Adam said, This is now bone of my bones, and flesh of my flesh: she shall be called Woman, because she was taken out of Man.
[24 NIV] For this reason a man will leave his father and mother and be united to his wife, and they will become one flesh.
[24 KJV] Therefore shall a man leave his father and his mother, and shall cleave unto his wife: and they shall be one flesh.
[25 NIV] The man and his wife were both naked, and they felt no shame.
[25 KJV] And they were both naked, the man and his wife, and were not ashamed.
[NIV]
a. [2] Or ceased; also in verse 3
b. [5] Or land; also in verse 6
c. [5] Or land; also in verse 6
d. [6] Or mist
e. [7] The Hebrew for man (adam) sounds like and may be related to the Hebrew for ground (adamah); it is also the name Adam (see Gen. 2:20).
f. [12] Or good; pearls
g. [13] Possibly southeast Mesopotamia
h. [20] Or the man
i. [21] Or took part of the man's side
j. [22] Or part
k. [23] The Hebrew for woman sounds like the Hebrew for man.

[2 KJV] And the woman said unto the serpent, We may eat of the fruit of the trees of the garden:

[12 NIV] The man said, "The woman you put here with me--she gave me some fruit from the tree, and I ate it."
[12 KJV] And the man said, The woman whom thou gavest to be with me, she gave me of the tree, and I did eat.
[13 NIV] Then the LORD God said to the woman, "What is this you have done?" The woman said, "The serpent deceived me, and I ate."
[13 KJV] And the LORD God said unto the woman, What is this that thou hast done? And the woman said, The serpent beguiled me, and I did eat.
[14 NIV] So the LORD God said to the serpent, "Because you have done this, "Cursed are you above all the livestock and all the wild animals! You will crawl on your belly and you will eat dust all the days of your life.
[14 KJV] And the LORD God said unto the serpent, Because thou hast done this, thou art cursed above all cattle, and above every beast of the field; upon thy belly shalt thou go, and dust shalt thou eat all the days of thy life:
[15 NIV] And I will put enmity between you and the woman, and between your offspring [a] and hers; he will crush [b] your head, and you will strike his heel."
[15 KJV] And I will put enmity between thee and the woman, and between thy seed and her seed; it shall bruise thy head, and thou shalt bruise his heel.
[16 NIV] To the woman he said, "I will greatly increase your pains in childbearing; with pain you will give birth to children. Your desire will be for your husband, and he will rule over you."
[16 KJV] Unto the woman he said, I will greatly multiply thy sorrow and thy conception; in sorrow thou shalt bring forth children; and thy desire shall be to thy husband, and he shall rule over thee.
[17 NIV] To Adam he said, "Because you listened to your wife and ate from the tree about which I commanded you, `You must not eat of it,' "Cursed is the ground because of you; through painful toil you will eat of it all the days of your life.
[17 KJV] And unto Adam he said, Because thou hast hearkened unto the voice of thy wife, and hast eaten of the tree, of which I commanded thee, saying, Thou shalt not eat of it: cursed is the ground for thy sake; in sorrow shalt thou eat of it all the days of thy life;
[18 NIV] It will produce thorns and thistles for you, and you will eat the plants of the field.
[18 KJV] Thorns also and thistles shall it bring forth to thee; and thou shalt eat the herb of the field;
[19 NIV] By the sweat of your brow you will eat your food until you return to the ground, since from it you were taken; for dust you are and to dust you will return."
[19 KJV] In the sweat of thy face shalt thou eat bread, till thou return unto the ground; for out of it wast thou taken: for dust thou art, and unto dust shalt thou return.

[20 KJV] And Adam called his wife's name Eve; because she was the mother of all living.

[21 KJV] Unto Adam also and to his wife did the LORD God make coats of skins, and clothed them.

[1 NIV] Adam [a] lay with his wife Eve, and she became pregnant and gave birth to Cain. [b] She said, "With the help of the LORD I have brought forth [c] a man."

[5 NIV] but on Cain and his offering he did not look with favor. So Cain was very angry, and his face was downcast.
[5 KJV] But unto Cain and to his offering he had not respect. And Cain was very wroth, and his countenance fell.
[6 NIV] Then the LORD said to Cain, "Why are you angry? Why is your face downcast?
[6 KJV] And the LORD said unto Cain, Why art thou wroth? and why is thy countenance fallen?
[7 NIV] If you do what is right, will you not be accepted? But if you do not do what is right, sin is crouching at your door; it desires to have you, but you must master it."
[7 KJV] If thou doest well, shalt thou not be accepted? and if thou doest not well, sin lieth at the door. And unto thee shall be his desire, and thou shalt rule over him.
[8 NIV] Now Cain said to his brother Abel, "Let's go out to the field." [d] And while they were in the field, Cain attacked his brother Abel and killed him.
[8 KJV] And Cain talked with Abel his brother: and it came to pass, when they were in the field, that Cain rose up against Abel his brother, and slew him.

[9 KJV] And the LORD said unto Cain, Where is Abel thy brother? And he said, I know not: Am I my brother's keeper?
[10 NIV] The LORD said, "What have you done? Listen! Your brother's blood cries out to me from the ground.
[10 KJV] And he said, What hast thou done? the voice of thy brother's blood crieth unto me from the ground.
[11 NIV] Now you are under a curse and driven from the ground, which opened its mouth to receive your brother's blood from your hand.
[11 KJV] And now art thou cursed from the earth, which hath opened her mouth to receive thy brother's blood from thy hand;
[12 NIV] When you work the ground, it will no longer yield its crops for you. You will be a restless wanderer on the earth."

[13 NIV] Cain said to the LORD, "My punishment is more than I can bear.
[13 KJV] And Cain said unto the LORD, My punishment is greater than I can bear.
[14 NIV] Today you are driving me from the land, and I will be hidden from your presence; I will be a restless wanderer on the earth, and whoever finds me will kill me."
[14 KJV] Behold, thou hast driven me out this day from the face of the earth; and from thy face shall I be hid; and I shall be a fugitive and a vagabond in the earth; and it shall come to pass, that every one that findeth me shall slay me.
[15 NIV] But the LORD said to him, "Not so [e] ; if anyone kills Cain, he will suffer vengeance seven times over." Then the LORD put a mark on Cain so that no one who found him would kill him.
[15 KJV] And the LORD said unto him, Therefore whosoever slayeth Cain, vengeance shall be taken on him sevenfold. And the LORD set a mark upon Cain, lest any finding him should kill him.
[16 NIV] So Cain went out from the LORD's presence and lived in the land of Nod, [f] east of Eden.
[16 KJV] And Cain went out from the presence of the LORD, and dwelt in the land of Nod, on the east of Eden.
[17 NIV] Cain lay with his wife, and she became pregnant and gave birth to Enoch. Cain was then building a city, and he named it after his son Enoch.
[17 KJV] And Cain knew his wife; and she conceived, and bare Enoch: and he builded a city, and called the name of the city, after the name of his son, Enoch.
[18 NIV] To Enoch was born Irad, and Irad was the father of Mehujael, and Mehujael was the father of Methushael, and Methushael was the father of Lamech.
[18 KJV] And unto Enoch was born Irad: and Irad begat Mehujael: and Mehujael begat Methusael: and Methusael begat Lamech.
[19 NIV] Lamech married two women, one named Adah and the other Zillah.
[19 KJV] And Lamech took unto him two wives: the name of the one was Adah, and the name of the other Zillah.
[20 NIV] Adah gave birth to Jabal; he was the father of those who live in tents and raise livestock.
[20 KJV] And Adah bare Jabal: he was the father of such as dwell in tents, and of such as have cattle.
[21 NIV] His brother's name was Jubal; he was the father of all who play the harp and flute.
[21 KJV] And his brother's name was Jubal: he was the father of all such as handle the harp and organ.

[10 NIV] God said to him, "Your name is Jacob, [d] but you will no longer be called Jacob; your name will be Israel. [e] " So he named him Israel.
[10 KJV] And God said unto him, Thy name is Jacob: thy name shall not be called any more Jacob, but Israel shall be thy name: and he called his name Israel.
[11 NIV] And God said to him, "I am God Almighty [f] ; be fruitful and increase in number. A nation and a community of nations will come from you, and kings will come from your body.
[11 KJV] And God said unto him, I am God Almighty: be fruitful and multiply; a nation and a company of nations shall be of thee, and kings shall come out of thy loins;
[12 NIV] The land I gave to Abraham and Isaac I also give to you, and I will give this land to your descendants after you."
[12 KJV] And the land which I gave Abraham and Isaac, to thee I will give it, and to thy seed after thee will I give the land.
[13 NIV] Then God went up from him at the place where he had talked with him.
[13 KJV] And God went up from him in the place where he talked with him.
[14 NIV] Jacob set up a stone pillar at the place where God had talked with him, and he poured out a drink offering on it; he also poured oil on it.
[14 KJV] And Jacob set up a pillar in the place where he talked with him, even a pillar of stone: and he poured a drink offering thereon, and he poured oil thereon.
[15 NIV] Jacob called the place where God had talked with him Bethel. [g]
[15 KJV] And Jacob called the name of the place where God spake with him, Bethel.
[16 NIV] Then they moved on from Bethel. While they were still some distance from Ephrath, Rachel began to give birth and had great difficulty.
[16 KJV] And they journeyed from Bethel; and there was but a little way to come to Ephrath: and Rachel travailed, and she had hard labour.
[17 NIV] And as she was having great difficulty in childbirth, the midwife said to her, "Don't be afraid, for you have another son."
[17 KJV] And it came to pass, when she was in hard labour, that the midwife said unto her, Fear not; thou shalt have this son also.
[18 NIV] As she breathed her last--for she was dying--she named her son Ben-Oni. [h] But his father named him Benjamin. [i]
[18 KJV] And it came to pass, as her soul was in departing, (for she died) that she called his name Benoni: but his father called him Benjamin.
[19 NIV] So Rachel died and was buried on the way to Ephrath (that is, Bethlehem).
[19 KJV] And Rachel died, and was buried in the way to Ephrath, which is Bethlehem.
[20 NIV] Over her tomb Jacob set up a pillar, and to this day that pillar marks Rachel's tomb.
[20 KJV] And Jacob set a pillar upon her grave: that is the pillar of Rachel's grave unto this day.
[21 NIV] Israel moved on again and pitched his tent beyond Migdal Eder.
[21 KJV] And Israel journeyed, and spread his tent beyond the tower of Edar.
[22 NIV] While Israel was living in that region, Reuben went in and slept with his father's concubine Bilhah, and Israel heard of it. Jacob had twelve sons:
[22 KJV] And it came to pass, when Israel dwelt in that land, that Reuben went and lay with Bilhah his father's concubine: and Israel heard it. Now the sons of Jacob were twelve:
[23 NIV] The sons of Leah: Reuben the firstborn of Jacob, Simeon, Levi, Judah, Issachar and Zebulun.
[23 KJV] The sons of Leah; Reuben, Jacob's firstborn, and Simeon, and Levi, and Judah, and Issachar, and Zebulun:
[24 NIV] The sons of Rachel: Joseph and Benjamin.
[24 KJV] The sons of Rachel; Joseph, and Benjamin:
[25 NIV] The sons of Rachel's maidservant Bilhah: Dan and Naphtali.
[25 KJV] And the sons of Bilhah, Rachel's handmaid; Dan, and Naphtali:
[26 NIV] The sons of Leah's maidservant Zilpah: Gad and Asher. These were the sons of Jacob, who were born to him in Paddan Aram.
[26 KJV] And the sons of Zilpah, Leah's handmaid; Gad, and Asher: these are the sons of Jacob, which were born to him in Padanaram.
[27 NIV] Jacob came home to his father Isaac in Mamre, near Kiriath Arba (that is, Hebron), where Abraham and Isaac had stayed.
[27 KJV] And Jacob came unto Isaac his father unto Mamre, unto the city of Arbah, which is Hebron, where Abraham and Isaac sojourned.
[28 NIV] Isaac lived a hundred and eighty years.
[28 KJV] And the days of Isaac were an hundred and fourscore years.

[1 NIV] This is the account of Esau (that is, Edom).

Chapter 38

[1 NIV] At that time, Judah left his brothers and went down to stay with a man of Adullam named Hirah.

[3 NIV] she became pregnant and gave birth to a son, who was named Er.

[15 KJV] And when Joseph's brethren saw that their father was dead, they said, Joseph will peradventure hate us, and will certainly requite us all the evil which we did unto him.
[16 NIV] So they sent word to Joseph, saying, "Your father left these instructions before he died:
[16 KJV] And they sent a messenger unto Joseph, saying, Thy father did command before he died, saying,
[17 NIV] `This is what you are to say to Joseph: I ask you to forgive your brothers the sins and the wrongs they committed in treating you so badly.' Now please forgive the sins of the servants of the God of your father." When their message came to him, Joseph wept.
[17 KJV] So shall ye say unto Joseph, Forgive, I pray thee now, the trespass of thy brethren, and their sin; for they did unto thee evil: and now, we pray thee, forgive the trespass of the servants of the God of thy father. And Joseph wept when they spake unto him.
[18 NIV] His brothers then came and threw themselves down before him. "We are your slaves," they said.
[18 KJV] And his brethren also went and fell down before his face; and they said, Behold, we be thy servants.
[19 NIV] But Joseph said to them, "Don't be afraid. Am I in the place of God?
[19 KJV] And Joseph said unto them, Fear not: for am I in the place of God?
[20 NIV] You intended to harm me, but God intended it for good to accomplish what is now being done, the saving of many lives.
[20 KJV] But as for you, ye thought evil against me; but God meant it unto good, to bring to pass, as it is this day, to save much people alive.
[21 NIV] So then, don't be afraid. I will provide for you and your children." And he reassured them and spoke kindly to them.
[21 KJV] Now therefore fear ye not: I will nourish you, and your little ones. And he comforted them, and spake kindly unto them.
[22 NIV] Joseph stayed in Egypt, along with all his father's family. He lived a hundred and ten years
[22 KJV] And Joseph dwelt in Egypt, he, and his father's house: and Joseph lived an hundred and ten years.
[23 NIV] and saw the third generation of Ephraim's children. Also the children of Makir son of Manasseh were placed at birth on Joseph's knees. [c]
[23 KJV] And Joseph saw Ephraim's children of the third generation: the children also of Machir the son of Manasseh were brought up upon Joseph's knees.
[24 NIV] Then Joseph said to his brothers, "I am about to die. But God will surely come to your aid and take you up out of this land to the land he promised on oath to Abraham, Isaac and Jacob."
[24 KJV] And Joseph said unto his brethren, I die: and God will surely visit you, and bring you out of this land unto the land which he sware to Abraham, to Isaac, and to Jacob.
[25 NIV] And Joseph made the sons of Israel swear an oath and said, "God will surely come to your aid, and then you must carry my bones up from this place."
[25 KJV] And Joseph took an oath of the children of Israel, saying, God will surely visit you, and ye shall carry up my bones from hence.
[26 NIV] So Joseph died at the age of a hundred and ten. And after they embalmed him, he was placed in a coffin in Egypt.
[26 KJV] So Joseph died, being an hundred and ten years old: and they embalmed him, and he was put in a coffin in Egypt.
